#新手教程
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> to move.=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 移动。
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> on your keyboard until the progress bar is filled!=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 按住键盘上的按键，直到进度条填满！
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> to move=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 移动
Use <b><u>LEFT MOUSE + RIGHT MOUSE</b></u> to rotate an object you are holding=使用 <b><u>鼠标左键+鼠标右键</b></u> 旋转你拿着的物品
<b>FOCUS > </b>Move to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>移动以填充进度条
<b>FOCUS > </b>Jump to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>跳跃以填充进度条
Press <u><b>SPACE</b></u> to jump.=按 <u><b>SPACE</b></u> 跳。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Sneak to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>蹲下填充进度条
Press <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> to sneak. Monsters are less likely to see you.=按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 蹲下，怪物可能看不到你。
Hold <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> and use <u><b>WASD</b></u> until the progess is filled!=长按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 和使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 直到进度完成！
Hold <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> and walk in under a prop, stay there until you fill the progress bar!=长按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 然后走进物体下面，呆在那里，直到你填满进度条！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Hide to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>躲藏以填充进度条
Use <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> to sneak under stuff and hide.=使用 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 偷偷溜到物体下面躲起来。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Sprint to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>冲刺以填充进度条
Hold down <u><b>LEFT SHIFT</b></u> to sprint. This drains your energy.=长按 <u><b>左 Shift</b></u> 冲刺，这会消耗你的耐力。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Run, jump and fall to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>奔跑、跳跃和翻滚以填充进度条
Run and press <u><b>Q</b></u> to fall with style. Jumping also helps!=奔跑并按下 <u><b>Q</b></u> 进行翻滚，也可以进行跳跃！
Run (<u><b>LEFT SHIFT</b></u>), jump (<u><b>SPACE</b></u>) and press <u><b>Q</b></u> to throw yourself. Do it until you fill the progress bar!=冲刺(<u><b>左 Shift</b></u>)，跳跃(<u><b>SPACE</b></u>)并按 <u><b>Q</b></u> 这样做，直到你填满进度条！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Carry that thing to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>携带该物品以填充进度条
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) and hold it until you fill the progress bar!=抓取(<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>)按住它，直到填满进度条！
Grab objects using <u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>.=使用<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>抓取物品.
<b>FOCUS > </b>Alter the distance of a grabbed item=<b>提示> </b>改变抓取物品的距离
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) an item and use <u><b>MOUSE SCROLL</b></u> to alter the distance of the item you grabbed!=抓住(<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>)物品 <u><b>滚动鼠标</b></u> 改变你抓取的物品的距离！
Use <u><b>MOUSE SCROLL</b></u> to alter the distance of grabbed objects.=使用 <u><b>鼠标滚动</b></u> 以改变抓取物品的距离。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Rotate stuff to fill the progress bar.=<b>提示> </b>旋转物品以填充进度条。
Rotate grabbed objects using <u><b>MOUSE RIGHT</b></u>.=使用以下按键旋转抓取的物品 <u><b>鼠标右键</b></u>.
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) and hold it while you press <u><b>MOUSE RIGHT</b></u> and move your aim to rotate it. Rotate until you fill the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>)按住它，同时按下 <u><b>鼠标右键</b></u> 然后移动并旋转它，旋转直到填满进度条！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Toggle that thing on and off.=<b>提示> </b>打开和关闭物品。
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) the ball and toggle it on and off using <u><b>E</b></u> until you fill the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>)然后使用以下按键打开和关闭球 <u><b>E</b></u> 直到你填满进度条！
Grab and press <u><b>E</b></u> to toggle items.=抓取并按下 <u><b>E</b></u> 进行物品交互。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill your entire inventory.=<b>提示> </b>装满您的全部库存。
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) an item, hold it and press <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u>. Fill all spots in your inventory to complete the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠标左键</b></u>)一个物品，按住它并按下 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u>键，装满库存中的所有位置以完成进度条！
Grab an Item and use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> to put it in your inventory.=抓取物品并按下 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 键把它放在你的库存中。
Use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> and empty all spots to fill the progress bar!=使用 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 并清空所有库存以填充进度条！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Empty your entire inventory.=<b>提示> </b>清空您的全部库存。
Use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> to take items out of your inventory.=使用 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 从库存中取出物品。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Check the map.=<b>提示> </b>查看地图。
Use <u><b>TAB</b></u> to view the map. The map is <b><u>important</b></u> for navigation.=使用 <u><b>Tab</b></u> 查看地图 <b><u>这很重要的</b></u>， 可用于导航。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Walk around with the C.A.R.T. a little.=<b>提示> </b>带着推车四处走走。
This is a C.A.R.T. Grab it by the handle.=这是推车，抓住把手。
C.A.R.T.=推车
Mode: STRONG=模式：强
<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill the C.A.R.T. with valuables.=<b>提示> </b>把贵重物品装满推车。
Fill C.A.R.T.s with valuables. C.A.R.T.s are <b><u>important</b></u> for carrying more stuff.=把贵重物品装满推车，推车 <b><u>很重要</b></u> 能携带更多物品。
Mode: WEAK=模式：弱
Put three items into the C.A.R.T.=将三个物品放入推车。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Extract the valuables.=<b>提示> </b>取出贵重物品。

<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill the extraction point with valuables=<b>提示> </b>在提取点装满贵重物品

###############################3.15翻译新增######################################################
REPO_HD=高清
Anti Aliasing=抗锯齿
REPO Scanner=扫描仪
REPO Config=模组配置
Sturdier Valuables=更坚固的贵重物品
The number of times the upgrade item is applied at the start of the game.=升级物品在游戏开始时应用的次数。
The maximum number of times the upgrade item can appear in the shop.=升级物品在商店中出现的最大次数。
The maximum number of times the upgrade item can be bought at once.=升级物品一次可购买的最大次数。
The initial delay (in seconds) before valuables begin scaling.=贵重物品开始缩放前的初始延迟（以秒为单位）。
The speed at which valuables scale down/up per update. Higher values make valuables shrink/expand faster.=贵重物品每次更新时缩放缩小/放大的速度。数值越高，贵重物品收缩/膨胀得越快。
Sets the time players have to kill a monster and get money when there aren’t enough items and the objectives are still pending.=当物品不足且目标仍未完成时，设置玩家击杀怪物并获得金钱的时间限制。
Ratio of Map Value to Extraction Goal. Ex: 20k map value to 10k goal is 2.0=地图价值与提取目标的比例。例如：20k地图价值对应10k目标为2.0。
The maximum number of health pacls the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 3=商店生成的生命补给包的最大数量。原版默认值为3。
The maximum number of upgrades the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 3=商店生成的升级物品的最大数量。原版默认值为3。
The maximum number of items the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 8=商店生成的物品的最大数量。原版默认值为8。
How fast descriptions scroll. (Seconds per character)=描述滚动的速度。（每秒字符数）
Description Scroll Speed=描述滚动速度
The multiplier of how much value is deducted from a hit (lower is better)=击中时价值扣除的倍数（越低越好）。
Damage Reduction Multiplier=伤害减免倍数。
Health amount deducted each time while crouching | 蹲下治疗扣除自己的生命值=蹲下治疗时每次扣除的生命值。
Health amount healed each time while crouching | 蹲下治疗治疗队友的生命值=蹲下治疗时每次治疗队友的生命值。
Interval for grab heal while crouching (in seconds) | 蹲下治疗的间隔时间（秒）=蹲下治疗的间隔时间（秒）。
You have more stamina, strength and can jump higher!\nPress R to continue=你拥有更多耐力、力量并能跳得更高！\n按R键继续

[H] Heal yourself for {{A}} health ({{B}} Mana)\n\n[N] Regenerate your stamina to full ({{C}} Mana)\n\n[J] Become faster for {{D}} seconds ({{E}} Mana)\n\n[O] Boost the effectivity of spells used in the next {{F}} seconds ({{G}} Mana)\n\n[K] Jump higher for {{H}} seconds ({{I}} Mana)=[H] 治疗自己{{A}}点生命值（消耗{{B}}点法力）\n\n[N] 完全恢复耐力（消耗{{C}}点法力）\n\n[J] 在{{D}}秒内提升速度（消耗{{E}}点法力）\n\n[O] 在接下来的{{F}}秒内提升法术效果（消耗{{G}}点法力）\n\n[K] 在{{H}}秒内跳得更高（消耗{{I}}点法力）

Sets healing value options to the same as in health packs, one of which will be applied randomly\rAttention! You must set the `PhaseMode` parameter to only one of `Level` or `Lobby`, not both. Otherwise, the healing will be done twice.\rIf the value is `None`, then it is disabled.\rIt has priority over the `Percent` and `ExactValue` parameters.\rFor example, if you set the value to `Medium, Large`, you will receive a random healing of 50HP or 100HP.\rSmall - heal 25 HP.\rMedium - heal 50 HP.\rLarge - heal 100 HP.=将治疗值选项设为与医疗包相同，并随机应用其中一种  \n注意！必须将 `PhaseMode` 参数仅设为 `Level` 或 `Lobby` 之一，不可同时设置，否则治疗会生效两次。  \n若值为 `None`，则禁用此功能。  \n该参数优先级高于 `Percent` 和 `ExactValue`。  \n例如：设为 `Medium, Large` 时，将随机恢复50HP或100HP。  \n- 小型：恢复25HP  \n- 中型：恢复50HP  \n- 大型：恢复100HP

Sets the exact value to heal.\rAttention! You must set the `PhaseMode` parameter to only one of `Level` or `Lobby`, not both. Otherwise, the healing will be done twice.\rIf the value is `0`, then it is disabled.\rIt has priority over the `Percent` parameter.\rFor example, if you set the value to `15`, you will always receive 15 HP.=设置精确的治疗数值。  \n注意！必须将 `PhaseMode` 参数仅设为 `Level` 或 `Lobby` 之一，不可同时设置，否则治疗会生效两次。  \n若值为 `0`，则禁用此功能。  \n该参数优先级高于 `Percent`。  \n例如：设为 `15` 时，将固定恢复15HP。

Configures in which phases of the game health restoration will be triggered.\rLevel - when spawning in the level.\rShop - when spawning in the shop. Attention! Healing in the store does not affect the game.\rLobby - when spawning in the truck (not menu) before starting the next level.\rAll - in all phases.=配置游戏在哪些阶段触发生命恢复：  \n**关卡** - 进入关卡时；  \n**商店** - 进入商店时（注意：商店内恢复不影响游戏进程）；  \n**准备区** - 进入卡车（非菜单）准备下一关时；  \n**全部** - 所有阶段均生效。
